##################################################################
# konfiguracios resz:
CFG:
    CPAR:
        P0 = TIMER_ERRC
        P1 = TIMER_CFGS
        P2 = TIMER_PRIO
        P3 = TIMER_LOGF
        P4 = TIMER_FLEN
        P5 = TIMER_LOGC
        P6 = TIMER_LOGM
        P7 = TIMER_CHKT
        P8 = TIMER_CNAM
        P9 = TIMER_ESEQ

CFGS = P1
PRIO = P2
LOGF = P3
FLEN = P4
LOGC = P5
LOGM = P6
CHKT = P7
CNAM = P8
ESEQ = P9


##------------------------------------------------------------------------------
## OBJECTS of Date-time
#
#OBJ:INIT_DATE_TIME
#    CPAR:
#       P0=SysClkSec
#    CFV:ELSE Q1;
#    TR0: SEC:1
#    OPAR:
#       P0= SysClkSec
#       P1= SysClkMin
#       P2= SysClkHour
#       P3= SysClkDay
#       P4= SysClkMonth
#       P5= SysClkYear
#       P6= SysClkDayOfWeek
#    OT:P0=SEC, P1=MIN, P2=HOUR, P3=DAY, P4=MONTH, P5=YEAR
#

##################################################################
# Change EVVIx_SLOT_FLAG (0->1 or 1->0) every day at 0:0:1
# to load normal/normal1 slot info so that Eventviewer goes to Online.
#
#OBJ: Evvi1_slot
#    TA: SEC:3, MIN:0, HOUR:0,
#    OPAR:
#        P0 = EVVI1_SLOT_FLAG
#    OFV0: P0 = ELSE 1-P0;
#
#OBJ: Evvi2_slot
#    TA: SEC:3, MIN:0, HOUR:0,
#    OPAR:
#        P0 = EVVI2_SLOT_FLAG
#    OFV0: P0 = ELSE 1-P0;
#
#OBJ: Evvi3_slot
#    TA: SEC:3, MIN:0, HOUR:0,
#    OPAR:
#        P0 = EVVI3_SLOT_FLAG
#    OFV0: P0 = ELSE 1-P0;
#
#OBJ: Evvi4_slot
#    TA: SEC:3, MIN:0, HOUR:0,
#    OPAR:
#        P0 = EVVI4_SLOT_FLAG
#    OFV0: P0 = ELSE 1-P0;
#
#OBJ: Evvi5_slot
#    TA: SEC:3, MIN:0, HOUR:0,

#        P0 = EVVI5_SLOT_FLAG
#    OFV0: P0 = ELSE 1-P0;
#

OBJ: cikl01_relativ
    CPAR:
        P0 = T_Cyc01Control
    CFV: IF P0 : Q1;  ELSE Q0;
    TPAR:
        P0 = T_Cyc01StartHour
        P1 = T_Cyc01StartMinute
        P2 = T_Cyc01CycleHour
        P3 = T_Cyc01CycleMinute
    TDA: SEC:0, MIN:P1, HOUR:P0,
    TR0: SEC:0, MIN:P3, HOUR:P2,
    OPAR:
        P0 = T_Cyc01Trigger
    OFVD: P0 = ELSE 1;
    OFV0: P0 = ELSE 1;

    OFV0:  P0 = ELSE 0;
